(function() {
  try {
    function getShortestColumn(colHeights) {
      var shortestIndex = 0;
      var minHeight = colHeights[0];
      for (var i = 1; i < colHeights.length; i++) {
        if (colHeights[i] < colHeights[shortestIndex]) {
          shortestIndex = i;
          minHeight = colHeights[i];
        }
      }
      return shortestIndex;
    }

    var oldGridPins = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName('static'));
    var newGridPins = [].slice.call(document.getElementsByClassName('Collection-Item-Measuring'));
    var pins = oldGridPins.concat(newGridPins);
    if (!pins.length) {
      return;
    }
    var grids = document.getElementsByClassName('gridCentered');
    if (!grids.length) {
      return;
    }
    var gridWidth = grids[0].getBoundingClientRect().width;
    var gapY = 16;
    var pinWidth = pins[0].getBoundingClientRect().width;
    var numCols = Math.floor(gridWidth / pinWidth);
    var colHeights = new Array(numCols).fill(0);

    var nextTop, nextLeft, shortestColumn, pin;

    for (var i = 0; i < pins.length; i++) {
      pin = pins[i];
      shortestColumn = getShortestColumn(colHeights);
      nextTop = colHeights[shortestColumn];
      nextLeft = shortestColumn * pinWidth;
      colHeights[shortestColumn] = colHeights[shortestColumn] + pin.clientHeight + gapY;

      pin.style.setProperty('top', nextTop + 'px', 'important');
      pin.style.setProperty('left', nextLeft + 'px', 'important');
      pin.style.setProperty('visibility', 'visible', 'important');
    }
  } catch (e) {}
})();
